  • Just the UI: Lots of people use React as the V in MVC. Since React makes no assumptions about the rest of your technology stack, itâ€™s easy to try it out on a small feature in an existing project.

  • Data flow: React implements one-way reactive data flow which reduces boilerplate and is easier to reason about than traditional data binding.

        "GET",
